## <a name="windows-server-2008-r2-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="59dda-1411">Windows Server 2008 R2-Attribute</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="59dda-1411">Windows Server 2008 R2 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="59dda-1412">Diese Klasse enthält die folgenden Attribute für Windows Server 2008 R2:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="59dda-1412">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008 R2:</span></span>
